href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%A0%A1%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6" title="斯特拉斯堡大学">斯特拉斯堡大学</a><br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8C%E7%88%BE%E7%A7%91%E6%8A%80%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8" title="里爾科技大學">里尔科技大学</a><br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E7%AD%89%E5%B8%AB%E7%AF%84%E5%AD%B8%E6%A0%A1%EF%BC%88%E5%B7%B4%E9%BB%8E%EF%BC%89" title="高等師範學校（巴黎）">巴黎高等师范学校</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="text-align:left;white-space:nowrap;;">著名學生</th><td style=""><a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%A5%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%94" title="查尔斯·弗里德尔">查尔斯·弗里德尔</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></td></tr><tr style="display:none"><td colspan="2">
</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">签名</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg"><img alt="Louis Pasteur Signature.svg" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="200" decoding="async" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg/150px-Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg/225px-Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg/300px-Louis_Pasteur_Signature.svg.png 2x" width="150"/></a></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>路易·巴斯德</b>（法語：<span lang="fr">Louis Pasteur</span>，<small>法语发音：</small><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r61209503">.mw-parser-output .IPA{font-family:"Charis SIL","Doulos SIL","Linux Libertine","Segoe UI","Lucida Sans Unicode","Code2000","Gentium","Gentium Alternative","TITUS Cyberbit Basic","Arial Unicode MS","IPAPANNEW","Chrysanthi Unicode","GentiumAlt","Bitstream Vera","Bitstream Cyberbit","Hiragino Kaku Gothic Pro","Lucida Grande",sans-serif;text-decoration:none!important}.mw-parser-output .IPA a:link,.mw-parser-output .IPA a:visited{text-decoration:none!important}</style><span class="IPA" title="国际音标"><a href="/wiki/Help:%E6%B3%95%E8%AA%9E%E5%9C%8B%E9%9A%9B%E9%9F%B3%E6%A8%99" title="Help:法語國際音標">[lwi pastœʁ]</a></span>，1822年12月27日－1895年9月28日），<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E5%9B%BD" title="法国">法国</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%A6" title="微生物学">微生物学</a>家、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6%E5%AE%B6" title="化学家">化学家</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%A6" title="微生物学">微生物学</a>的奠基人之一。他以借<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E6%BA%90%E8%AF%B4" title="生源说">生源说</a>否定<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E8%AF%B4" title="自然发生说">自然发生说</a>（自生说）、倡导<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85%E7%BB%86%E8%8F%8C%E5%AD%A6%E8%AF%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="疾病细菌学说（页面不存在）">疾病细菌学说</a>（胚种学说），以及发明<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A0%90%E9%98%B2%E6%8E%A5%E7%A8%AE" title="預防接種">预防接种</a>方法以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%B0%8F%E7%81%AD%E8%8F%8C%E6%B3%95" title="巴氏灭菌法">巴氏杀菌法</a>而闻名，為第一個創造<a href="/wiki/%E7%8B%82%E7%8A%AC%E7%97%85" title="狂犬病">狂犬病</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%82%AD%E7%96%BD%E7%97%85" title="炭疽病">炭疽病</a><a href="/wiki/%E7%96%AB%E8%8B%97" title="疫苗">疫苗</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="科學家">科學家</a>。被世人称颂为 “进入科学王国的最完美无缺的人”<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dubos_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-dubos-2">[2]</a></sup>。他和<a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%B9%E8%BF%AA%E5%8D%97%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E7%A7%91%E6%81%A9" title="费迪南德·科恩">费迪南德·科恩</a>以及<a href="/wiki/%E7%BD%97%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E7%A7%91%E8%B5%AB" title="罗伯特·科赫">罗伯特·科赫</a>一起开创了<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%8F%8C%E5%AD%B8" title="細菌學">细菌学</a>，被认为是<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%A6" title="微生物学">微生物学</a>的奠基者之一<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kepu_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-kepu-3">[3]</a></sup>，常被稱为“微生物學之父”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-catholic_intro_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-catholic_intro-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fein_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-fein-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-van_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-van-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p><p>2005年，法国国家二台举行了“<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%80%E5%81%89%E5%A4%A7%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%9C%8B%E4%BA%BA" title="最偉大的法國人">最伟大的法国人</a>”的评选活动，结果巴斯德名列第二位，仅次于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8F%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E6%88%B4%E9%AB%98%E4%B9%90" title="夏尔·戴高乐">夏尔·戴高乐</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="zh"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">目录</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span id=".E7.94.9F.E5.B9.B3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="生平">生平</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：生平">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2048" data-file-width="1536" decoding="async" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg/150px-Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg/225px-Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg/300px-Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Pasteur_Geburtshaus_in_Dole.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>位于<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%9A%E5%B0%94_(%E6%B1%9D%E6%8B%89%E7%9C%81)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="多尔 (汝拉省)（页面不存在）">多尔</a>的巴斯德出生时的住宅。</div></div></div>
<p>巴斯德于1822年生于法国东部<a href="/wiki/%E6%B1%9D%E6%8B%89%E7%9C%81" title="汝拉省">汝拉省</a>城市<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E5%8B%92" title="多勒">多勒</a>。他父親是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8B%BF%E7%A0%B4%E5%B4%99" title="拿破崙">拿破崙</a>軍骑兵队的一名退伍軍人，後成為皮鞋匠，家境並不富裕。巴斯德出生2月后，他们家就搬迁到<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%B0%94%E5%B8%83%E7%93%A6" title="阿尔布瓦">阿尔布瓦</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-catholic_intro_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-catholic_intro-4">[4]</a></sup>。他在1839年-1842年在<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%9D%E6%A1%91%E6%9D%BE%E7%9A%87%E5%AE%B6%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="贝桑松皇家学院（页面不存在）">贝桑松皇家学院</a>学习，并开始对科学感兴趣。由于对科学的兴趣，巴斯德从1843年-1846年在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E7%AD%89%E5%B8%AB%E7%AF%84%E5%AD%B8%E6%A0%A1%EF%BC%88%E5%B7%B4%E9%BB%8E%EF%BC%89" title="高等師範學校（巴黎）">巴黎高等师范学校</a>学习，1845年获硕士学位，1847年获博士学位毕业。他于1848年开始任<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%AC%AC%E6%88%8E%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="第戎大学（页面不存在）">第戎大学</a>物理学教授，后在1849年转至<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%A0%A1%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6" title="斯特拉斯堡大学">斯特拉斯堡大学</a>理学院任化学教授<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-中国大百科全书_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-中国大百科全书-8">[8]</a></sup>。在那里，巴斯德遇到了他的妻子并于1849年5月29日結婚。巴斯德共有过5個子女中，只有兩個活到成年，而其餘三個死於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%82%B7%E5%AF%92" title="傷寒">傷寒</a>，此事激發了他去研究治癒各種<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%A0%E6%9F%93%E7%97%85" title="传染病">传染病</a>的方法。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-catholic_intro_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-catholic_intro-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-past_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-past-9">[9]</a></sup>他在1868年首次<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E9%A2%A8" title="中風">中風</a>，1887年再次中風。1895年9月28日卒於巴黎，享壽72歲。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-liao_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-liao-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6.E7.BB.8F.E5.8E.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="研究经历">研究经历</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：研究经历">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="492" decoding="async" height="183" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg/150px-Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg/225px-Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg/300px-Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tableau_Louis_Pasteur.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>路易·巴斯德在实验室工作，<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%B0%94%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E5%9F%83%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%94%E8%B4%B9%E5%B0%94%E7%89%B9" title="阿尔伯特·埃德尔费尔特">阿尔伯特·埃德尔费尔特</a>绘於1885年。</div></div></div>
<p>巴斯德于1854年-1857年任<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8C%E7%88%BE%E7%A7%91%E6%8A%80%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8" title="里爾科技大學">里尔科技大学</a>理学院院长和化学教授，1857年-1867年任巴黎高师的主管行政管理和科学研究的主任，于1862年被选为<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E5%9B%BD%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2" title="法国科学院">法国科学院</a>院士，1863年-1867年兼任<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B7%B4%E9%BB%8E%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E5%AD%A6%E6%A0%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="巴黎美术学校（页面不存在）">巴黎美术学校</a>教授，1867年-1874年任<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E9%BB%8E%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6" title="巴黎大学">巴黎大学</a>化学教授，1869年成为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E5%9B%BD%E7%9A%87%E5%AE%B6%E5%AD%A6%E4%BC%9A" title="英国皇家学会">英国皇家学会</a>会员，1867年-1888年任高等师范学校生理化学实验室主任，1882年被选为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B0%E8%A5%BF%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2_(%E6%9C%BA%E6%9E%84)" title="法兰西学院 (机构)">法兰西学院</a>院士，1887年被选为法国科学院永久秘书，1888年-1895年任<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="巴斯德研究所">巴斯德研究所</a>所长。1892年，巴黎大学为庆祝巴斯德70寿辰举行了盛大的国际性庆典。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-中国大百科全书_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-中国大百科全书-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6.E8.B4.A1.E7.8C.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="研究贡献">研究贡献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：研究贡献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.88.86.E5.AD.90.E5.AF.B9.E7.A7.B0.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="分子对称性">分子对称性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：分子对称性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pcrystals.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="230" data-file-width="288" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Pcrystals.svg/150px-Pcrystals.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Pcrystals.svg/225px-Pcrystals.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Pcrystals.svg/300px-Pcrystals.svg.png 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pcrystals.svg" title="放大"></a></div>巴斯德发现酒石酸有两种晶体，分别产生<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%B3%E6%97%8B" title="右旋">右旋</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%A6%E6%97%8B" title="左旋">左旋</a>现象。</div></div></div>
<p>早期的巴斯德是一名化學家，还在大学时代，巴斯德便开始了对化学结晶体形态和结构的研究。当时，人们发现从生物合成的酒石酸会令<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%8F%E6%8C%AF%E5%85%89" title="偏振光">平面偏振光</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%B3%E6%97%8B" title="右旋">右旋</a>的，但是<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6%E5%90%88%E6%88%90" title="化学合成">化学合成</a>得到的酒石酸（异酒石酸）却没有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%8B%E5%85%89%E6%80%A7" title="旋光性">旋光性</a>，但是化学分析表明，这两种途径得到的酒石酸的化学反应和元素构成都是一模一样的。通过<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%98%BE%E5%BE%AE%E9%95%9C" title="显微镜">显微镜</a>的观察，他发现化学合成的异酒石酸裡实际上包含了两种晶体。一种就是常见的右旋的酒石酸，另一种则是左旋的。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%96%E6%B6%88%E6%97%8B%E4%BD%93" title="外消旋体">两种晶体的混合</a>后，使得旋光性消失。巴斯德在1848年发表了他的发现<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>。这一发现证实了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%8B%E5%85%89%E5%BC%82%E6%9E%84%E4%BD%93" title="旋光异构体">旋光异构体</a>的设想，对<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E6%9E%84%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6" title="结构化学">结构化学</a>的发展具有重要影响。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gal_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-Gal-15">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-xie_ch24_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-xie_ch24-16">[16]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lu_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-lu-17">[17]</a></sup>巴斯德以后又提出了<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%88%86%E5%AD%90%E4%B8%8D%E5%AF%B9%E7%A7%B0%E6%80%A7%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="分子不对称性理论（页面不存在）">分子不对称性理论</a>，开创了<a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%8B%E4%BD%93%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6" title="立体化学">立体化学</a>研究的途径。他还发现生物体对这两种不对称性的晶体具有明显的选择性。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.91.E9.85.B5.E7.9A.84.E7.BB.86.E8.8F.8C.E7.90.86.E8.AE.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="发酵的细菌理论">发酵的细菌理论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：发酵的细菌理论">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">更多信息：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E8%AF%B4" title="自然发生说">自然發生說</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1547" decoding="async" height="228" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg/220px-Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg/330px-Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg/440px-Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Pasteur_experiment.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>巴斯德在实验室里做实验。</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Coldecygne.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="439" data-file-width="655" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Coldecygne.svg/220px-Coldecygne.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Coldecygne.svg/330px-Coldecygne.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Coldecygne.svg/440px-Coldecygne.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Coldecygne.svg" title="放大"></a></div>巴斯德使用过的<a href="/wiki/%E9%B9%85%E9%A2%88%E7%93%B6" title="鹅颈瓶">鹅颈瓶</a></div></div></div>
<p>法国的<a href="/wiki/%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E9%85%92" title="葡萄酒">葡萄酒</a>业非常有名，但是久置的啤酒和葡萄酒会变酸。<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8C%E5%B0%94" title="里尔">里尔</a>酿酒商向巴斯德请教如何防止让酒变酸。巴斯德首先研究了酒的发酵过程。他发现发酵是因为<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="微生物">微生物</a>（<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D%E8%8F%8C" title="酵母菌">酵母菌</a>）的增长造成的。酒变酸和发酵类似，不过是由不同的微生物引起的。巴斯德的发现改变了以往认为微生物是发酵的产物，发酵是一个纯粹的化学变化过程的错误观点。同时，巴斯德通过大量实验提出：环境、温度、pH值和基质的成分等因素的改变，以及有毒物质都以特有的方式影响着不同的微生物。他随后创立了“<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7%E6%B6%88%E6%AF%92%E6%B3%95" title="巴斯德消毒法">巴斯德消毒法</a>”（60~65摄氏度作短时间加热处理，杀死有害微生物的一种消毒法）并应用在各种食物和饮料上。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-中国大百科全书_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-中国大百科全书-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lu_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-lu-17">[17]</a></sup>
</p><p>1862年，巴斯德經多次實驗，終於以<a href="/wiki/%E9%B9%85%E9%A2%88%E7%93%B6" title="鹅颈瓶">鹅颈瓶</a>進行實驗，證明煮沸的肉湯內，不會增長細菌；因此否定認為「生物隨時可由非生物發生」的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E8%AF%B4" title="自然发生说">自然發生說</a>（無生源論、自生論）。他提出「一切生物來自生物」的結論（即生源論）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup>，是第一位了解微生物存在於食物中及其作用的科學家。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.8D.E7.96.AB.E5.AD.A6.E5.92.8C.E7.96.AB.E8.8B.97"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="免疫学和疫苗">免疫学和疫苗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：免疫学和疫苗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>除了發現防止紅酒變酸的方法之外，巴斯德也找到了導致蠶生病的原因。他的研究成果捍衛法國在絲織產業與時尚工業的優勢地位，這又是一樁足以令全法國人向他致敬的傑出成就。他接着將研究範圍拓展到家禽、家畜與人類疾病作用的方式，更透過研究疫苗證實其功效。巴斯德提出了预防接种措施，认为传染病的微生物在特殊的培养之下可以减轻毒力，变成防病的疫苗。他于1881年著手研究狂犬病，1885年以減毒的方式（the method for attenuatio of virulent microorganisms）研製出減毒狂犬病疫苗，巴斯德的名聲引來大西洋彼岸的求助，當時美國新澤西幾名男童遭到感染狂犬病的犬隻攻擊，性命垂危。這起新聞引起美國民眾的重視，自發集資協助這幾名男童跨越大西洋至巴黎，尋求巴斯德的救助，而巴斯德也不負眾望，利用他研究出的狂犬病疫苗，在同年7月6日治療一受狂犬咬傷的9歲兒童<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joseph Meister" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Joseph Meister"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Joseph_Meister&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Joseph Meister（页面不存在）">Joseph Meister</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Meister" title="en:Joseph Meister"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joseph Meister</span></a></span>）</span></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-中国大百科全书_8-3"><a href="#cite_note-中国大百科全书-8">[8]</a></sup>至此，巴斯德已經是跨越歐陸國界及大西洋隔閡的知識英雄。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.BF.A1.E4.BB.B0.E5.92.8C.E7.81.B5.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="信仰和灵性">信仰和灵性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：信仰和灵性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>天主教的观察者经常说巴斯德一生都是虔诚的<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E5%BE%92" title="基督徒">基督徒</a>。巴斯德的女婿在他为巴斯德所写的传记中也写过：
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r61209892">.mw-parser-output .templatequote{margin-top:0;overflow:hidden}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite{line-height:1em;text-align:left;padding-left:2em;margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite cite{font-size:small}</style>
</p>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>他完全相信上帝和永恒，深信今世赋予我们从善的力量将一直持续至来世，这种感情贯穿在巴斯德的整个生活当中。他念念不忘《新约》的福音所阐明的德行教条。就在自己生命的最后几周里，巴斯德对先人的宗教仪式充满了敬意。他朴素而自然的以这种仪式作精神支柱。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VR_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-VR-19">[19]</a></sup></p></blockquote>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Maurice Vallery-Radot" data-lang-code="fr" data-lang-name="法语" data-orig-title="莫里斯·瓦莱里-拉多"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8E%AB%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E7%93%A6%E8%8E%B1%E9%87%8C-%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="莫里斯·瓦莱里-拉多（页面不存在）">莫里斯·瓦莱里-拉多</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">法语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maurice_Vallery-Radot" title="fr:Maurice Vallery-Radot"><span dir="auto" lang="fr">Maurice Vallery-Radot</span></a></span>）</span></span>是巴斯德女婿兄弟的外孙，也是天主教徒。他也坚持巴斯德深信天主教。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>有一个被巴斯德·瓦莱里-拉多和莫里斯·瓦莱里-拉多证明是假的所谓巴斯德的话：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup>"The more I know, the more nearly is my faith that of the Breton peasant. Could I but know all I would have the faith of a Breton peasant's wife".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-catholic_intro_4-3"><a href="#cite_note-catholic_intro-4">[4]</a></sup>根据莫里斯·瓦莱里-拉多，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>这个错误的传言最早是在巴斯德时候不久出现的。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>但巴斯德的外孙<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Louis Pasteur Vallery-Radot" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="路易斯·巴斯德·瓦莱里-拉多"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E7%93%A6%E8%8E%B1%E9%87%8C-%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="路易斯·巴斯德·瓦莱里-拉多（页面不存在）">路易斯·巴斯德·瓦莱里-拉多</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Pasteur_Vallery-Radot" title="en:Louis Pasteur Vallery-Radot"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Louis Pasteur Vallery-Radot</span></a></span>）</span></span>说，巴斯德仅仅相信<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A9%E4%B8%BB%E6%95%99" title="天主教">天主教</a>中的灵性，但没有参加过日常的宗教活动，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup>尽管巴斯德信仰上帝，一般说，他的观点更接近自由思想家而不是天主教，他表现更多地是灵性的而不是宗教的。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup>巴斯德也反对将科学和宗教混在一起。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.AF.B9.E5.B7.B4.E6.96.AF.E5.BE.B7.E7.9A.84.E6.8C.87.E6.8E.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="对巴斯德的指控">对巴斯德的指控</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：对巴斯德的指控">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>1995年，在巴斯德逝世百年纪念之际，美国<a href="/wiki/%E6%99%AE%E6%9E%97%E6%96%AF%E9%A1%BF%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6" title="普林斯顿大学">普林斯顿大学</a><a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%8F%B2" title="科学史">科学史</a>教授<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Gerald L. Geison" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="拉尔德·盖森"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8B%89%E5%B0%94%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E7%9B%96%E6%A3%AE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="拉尔德·盖森（页面不存在）">拉尔德·盖森</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gerald_L._Geison" title="en:Gerald L. Geison"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Gerald L. Geison</span></a></span>）</span></span>出版了《巴斯德的隐秘科学》（The Private Science of Louis Pasteur）一书。书中声称，巴斯德这位“最完美无缺的科学家”有欺骗行为，巴斯德的实验记录有的不符合他公开的说法，并且他还从事了违反医学伦理的试验。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup>《<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BD%E7%BA%A6%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%A5" title="纽约时报">纽约时报</a>》立刻报道了该书的出版。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>1962年<a href="/wiki/%E8%AF%BA%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6%E5%A5%96" title="诺贝尔化学奖">诺贝尔化学奖</a>得主<a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E4%BD%A9%E9%B2%81%E8%8C%A8" title="马克斯·佩鲁茨">佩鲁茨</a>在《<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BD%E7%BA%A6%E4%B9%A6%E8%AF%84" title="纽约书评">纽约书评</a>》上发布文章《为先驱辩护》进行详细的反驳。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-perutz_33-0"><a href="#cite_note-perutz-33">[33]</a></sup>此后，相关争论一直不断。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fang_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-fang-36">[36]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.B7.B4.E6.96.AF.E5.BE.B7.E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6.E6.89.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="巴斯德研究所">巴斯德研究所</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：巴斯德研究所">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="巴斯德研究所">巴斯德研究所</a></div>
<p>1887年，巴斯德在巴黎以募捐方式创立了一所公益型私人研究所——<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="巴斯德研究所">巴斯德研究所</a>。建立之初，研究所规模很小，第一批研究队伍仅设5个实验室，有5位室主任和14位助手。至2005年，巴斯德研究所拥有一所医院。该所既是传染性疾病、热带病理学和免疫系统疾病的专业保健中心，又是研究生教育（科研和临床培训）中心，生物学基础研究中心、公共健康应用研究中心。同时它还建有一个博物馆、一个包括图书馆在内的科技信息中心、多家公司和分布在全球29个国家内的32所研究机构。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-yang_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-yang-38">[38]</a></sup> 共有8位诺贝尔生理学和医学奖获得者在该所学习和工作过，他们是<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8F%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E6%96%B9%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%8B%89%E9%9F%A6%E6%9C%97" title="夏尔·路易·阿方斯·拉韦朗">拉韦朗</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9E%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E5%A5%91%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%AF%E5%A4%AB" title="伊利亞·梅契尼可夫">梅契尼科夫</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%B1%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E5%8D%9A%E7%88%BE%E4%BB%A3" title="朱爾·博爾代">博尔代</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8F%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%B0%BC%E7%A7%91%E5%8B%92" title="夏尔·尼科勒">尼科尔</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E8%BE%BE%E5%B0%BC%E5%9F%83%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%8D%9A%E9%9F%A6" title="达尼埃尔·博韦">博韦</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%89%E5%BE%B7%E5%88%97%C2%B7%E5%88%A9%E6%B2%83%E5%A4%AB" title="安德列·利沃夫">利沃夫</a>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BC%97%E6%9C%97%E7%B4%A2%E7%93%A6%C2%B7%E9%9B%85%E5%90%84%E5%B8%83" title="弗朗索瓦·雅各布">雅各布</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B4%BE%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E8%8E%AB%E8%AF%BA" title="贾克·莫诺">莫诺</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-yang_38-1"><a href="#cite_note-yang-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.A7.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-VR-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-VR_19-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">（法）R.瓦莱里-拉多. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210423154534/http://book.ln.chaoxing.com/ebook/detail_10720429.html" rel="nofollow">微生物学的奠基人：巴斯德</a>. 商务印书馆. 1985: 488 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2013-10-17</span>]</span>. （<a class="external text" href="http://book.ln.chaoxing.com/ebook/detail_10720429.html" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2021-04-23）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=%EF%BC%88%E6%B3%95%EF%BC%89R.%E7%93%A6%E8%8E%B1%E9%87%8C-%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%9A&amp;rft.btitle=%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%A5%A0%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9A%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.date=1985&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=488&amp;rft.pub=%E5%95%86%E5%8A%A1%E5%8D%B0%E4%B9%A6%E9%A6%86&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fbook.ln.chaoxing.com%2Febook%2Fdetail_10720429.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-20"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-20">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Vallery-Radot, Maurice. Pasteur. Paris: Perrin. 1994: 377–407.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.aufirst=Maurice&amp;rft.aulast=Vallery-Radot&amp;rft.btitle=Pasteur&amp;rft.date=1994&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=377-407&amp;rft.place=Paris&amp;rft.pub=Perrin&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-21">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Pasteur Vallery-Radot, Letter to Paul Dupuy, 1939, quoted by Hilaire Cuny, <i>Pasteur et le mystère de la vie</i>, Paris, Seghers, 1963, p. 53–54.</span>

<li id="cite_note-22"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-22">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>Pasteur</i>, 1994, p. 378.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-23"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-23">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In Pasteur's <i>Semaine religieuse .... du diocèse de Versailles</i>, October 6, 1895, p. 153.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-24"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-24">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Pasteur Vallery-Radot, Letter to Paul Dupuy, 1939, quoted by Hilaire Cuny, <i>Pasteur et le mystère de la vie</i>, Paris, Seghers, 1963, p. 53–54. Patrice Pinet, <i>Pasteur et la philosophie</i>, Paris, 2005, p. 134–135, quotes analogous assertions of Pasteur Vallery-Radot, with references to Pasteur Vallery-Radot, <i>Pasteur inconnu</i>, p. 232, and André George, <i>Pasteur</i>, Paris, 1958, p. 187. According to Maurice Vallery-Radot (<i>Pasteur</i>, 1994, p. 378), the false quotation appeared for the first time in the <i>Semaine religieuse .... du diocèse de Versailles</i>, October 6, 1895, p. 153, shortly after the death of Pasteur.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-25"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-25">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Joseph McCabe. <a class="external text" href="https://www.infidels.org/library/historical/joseph_mccabe/dictionary.html" rel="nofollow">A Biographical Dictionary of Ancient, Medieval, and Modern Freethinkers</a>. Haldeman-Julius Publications. 1945 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2012-08-11</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://www.webcitation.org/6FKlqP9mW?url=http://www.infidels.org/library/historical/joseph_mccabe/dictionary.html" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2013-03-23）. <q>The anonymous Catholic author quotes as his authority the standard biography by Vallery-Radot, yet this describes Pasteur as a freethinker; and this is confirmed in the preface to the English translation by Sir W. Osler, who knew Pasteur personally. Vallery-Radot was himself a Catholic yet admits that Pasteur believed only in "an Infinite" and "hoped" for a future life. Pasteur publicly stated this himself in his Academy speech in 1822 (in V.R.). He said: "The idea of God is a form of the idea of the Infinite whether it is called Brahma, Allah, Jehova, or Jesus." The biographer says that in his last days he turned to the Church but the only "evidence" he gives is that he liked to read the life of St. Vincent de Paul, and he admits that he did not receive the sacraments at death. Relatives put rosary beads in his hands, and the Catholic Encyclopedia claims him as a Catholic in virtue of the fact and of an anonymous and inconclusive statement about him. Wheeler says in his Dictionary of Freethinkers that in his prime Pasteur was Vice-President of the British Secular (Atheist) Union; and Wheeler was the chief Secularist writer of the time. The evidence is overwhelming. Yet the Catholic scientist Sir Bertram Windle assures his readers that "no person who knows anything about him can doubt the sincerity of his attachment to the Catholic Church," and all Catholic writers use much the same scandalous language.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=Joseph+McCabe&amp;rft.btitle=A+Biographical+Dictionary+of+Ancient%2C+Medieval%2C+and+Modern+Freethinkers&amp;rft.date=1945&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pub=Haldeman-Julius+Publications&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.infidels.org%2Flibrary%2Fhistorical%2Fjoseph_mccabe%2Fdictionary.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-26"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-26">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Patrice Debré. Louis Pasteur. JHU Press. 2000: 176. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9780801865299" title="Special:网络书源/9780801865299"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9780801865299</a>. <q>Does this mean that Pasteur was bound to a religious ideal? His attitude was that of a believer, not of a sectarian. One of his most brilliant disciples, Elie Metchnikoff, was to attest that he spoke of religion only in general terms. In fact, Pasteur evaded the question by claiming quite simply that religion has no more place in science than science has in religion. ...A biologist more than a chemist, a spiritual more than a religious man, Pasteur was held back only by the lack of more powerful technical means and therefore had to limit himself to identifying germs and explaining their generation.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=Patrice+Debr%C3%A9&amp;rft.btitle=Louis+Pasteur&amp;rft.date=2000&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9780801865299&amp;rft.pages=176&amp;rft.pub=JHU+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-27"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-27">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Brendon Barnett. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20121114074938/http://www.pasteurbrewing.com/Articles/life-of-pasteur/louis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html" rel="nofollow">Louis Pasteur: A Religious Man?</a>. Pasteur Brewing. 2011-05-31 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2012-08-11</span>]</span>. （<a class="external text" href="http://www.pasteurbrewing.com/Articles/life-of-pasteur/louis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2012-11-14）. <q>However, unlike many others, Pasteur asserted the preeminence of hypotheses over religious or metaphysical prejudices and always seemed willing to abandon theories that were outdated or useless in practicality. Pasteur often saw religion as a hinderance to scientific progress. In 1874, presiding over the award ceremony at the Collège of Arbois, he clearly stated his position: "I know that the word free thinker is written somewhere within our walls as a challenge and an affront. Do you know what most of the free thinkers want? Some want the freedom not to think at all and to be fettered by ignorance; others want the freedom to think badly; and others still, the freedom to be dominated by what is suggested to them by instinct and to despise all authority and all tradition. Freedom of thought in the Cartesian sense, freedom to work hard, freedom to pursue research, the right to arrive at such truth as is accessible to evidence and to conform one's conduct to these exigencies--oh! let us vow a cult to this freedom; for this is what has created modern society in its highest and most fruitful aspects." Pasteur had great respect for the unknown and the infinite, but did not allow himself to become a victim of superstition and fanatical religious explanations.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=Brendon+Barnett&amp;rft.btitle=Louis+Pasteur%3A+A+Religious+Man%3F&amp;rft.date=2011-05-31&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.pub=Pasteur+Brewing&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.pasteurbrewing.com%2FArticles%2Flife-of-pasteur%2Flouis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-28"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-28">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Brendon Barnett. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20121114074938/http://www.pasteurbrewing.com/Articles/life-of-pasteur/louis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html" rel="nofollow">Louis Pasteur: A Religious Man?</a>. Pasteur Brewing. 2011-05-31 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2012-08-11</span>]</span>. （<a class="external text" href="http://www.pasteurbrewing.com/Articles/life-of-pasteur/louis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2012-11-14）. <q>Louis Pasteur did not deny religion, but was compelled to say that, "religion has no more place in science than science has in religion." The role of religion in his mind was clear: "In each one of us there are two men, the scientist and the man of faith or of doubt. These two spheres are separate, and woe to those who want to make them encroach upon one another in the present state of our knowledge!"</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=Brendon+Barnett&amp;rft.btitle=Louis+Pasteur%3A+A+Religious+Man%3F&amp;rft.date=2011-05-31&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.pub=Pasteur+Brewing&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.pasteurbrewing.com%2FArticles%2Flife-of-pasteur%2Flouis-pasteur-a-religious-man.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-29"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-29">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Patrice Debré. Louis Pasteur. JHU Press. 2000: 176. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9780801865299" title="Special:网络书源/9780801865299"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9780801865299</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E6%96%AF%E5%BE%B7&amp;rft.au=Patrice+Debr%C3%A9&amp;rft.btitle=Louis+Pasteur&amp;rft.date=2000&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9780801865299&amp;rft.pages=176&amp;rft.pub=JHU+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-30"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-30">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Gerald Geison. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/privatescienceof0000geis" rel="nofollow">The Private Science of Louis Pasteur</a>. <li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation news">Lewis Wolpert. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/1995/05/07/books/experiments-in-deceit.html?pagewanted=all&amp;src=pm" rel="nofollow">Experiments in Deceit</a>.
